<tr><td width="742"><h3><a href="https://github.com/1992513/djy/blob/master/gb/24/9/17/n14332919.md#1" target="_blank">加州房主正失去保险 立法者如何解决</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/1992513/djy/blob/master/gb/24/9/17/n14332919.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2024/09/id14332925-GettyImages-2163045217-1080x720-1-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>

作者：Siyamak Khorrami／张纯之编译
